â”‚ After removing autoplay from both AnalyticsStage and AnalyticsChart, nothing is visible. This means the animations never trigger at all.

Key insight: I assumed AnimatedFloatingElement would automatically trigger child useAnimation instances, but that's likely wrong.

useAnimation needs to be explicitly told to play() - either via:
1. Autoplay (which I removed)
2. Manual play() calls
3. Some other trigger mechanism

I need to understand:
- How AnimatedFloatingElement works
- How other working theaters handle this
- What triggers the animations if not autoplay

Let me hypothesize what's happening:
- AnimatedFloatingElement handles its own visibility/teleportation
- But it doesn't automatically trigger child useAnimation instances
- Those instances need their own trigger mechanism
- Removing autoplay removed the ONLY trigger   â”‚
